Qwf2Db-MnozTc-OWXEXe-MnozTc-wNfPc">Try Gemini Enterprise Business Edition today</h5><p class="nRhiJb-cHYyed Mrfygc nRhiJb-BP2Omd-ma6Yeb-KE6vqe nRhiJb-DbgRPb-R6PoUb-cGMI2b">The front door to AI in the workplace</p><a class="nRhiJb-LgbsSe  nRhiJb-LgbsSe-OWXEXe-CNusmb-o6Shpd " href="https://business.gemini.google/?utm_source=cloud.google.com/blog&amp;utm_medium=et&amp;utm_campaign=FY26-Q2-GLOBAL-GLO27877-physicalevent-er-next26-mc-105752" track-metadata-module="left now </a></div></div><div class="OYL9D nRhiJb-kR0ZEf-OWXEXe-GV1x9e-OiUrBf" jsname="tx2NYc"><section class="Wy08Ac nRhiJb-qJTHM-OWXEXe-hJDwNd nRhiJb-DbgRPb-II5mzb-cGMI2b"><div jsaction="rcuQ6b:npT2md" jscontroller="M0Q3Qb" data-is-cws-richtext="true" class=" "><p><span style="vertical-align:baseline">At Google Cloud, we continue to make critical investments to Vertex AI </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/agent-builder?e=48754805&amp;hl=en"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">Agent Builder</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline">, our comprehensive and open platform, enabling you to build faster, scale efficiently, and govern with enterprise-grade security.</span></p>
<p><span style="vertical-align:baseline">Today, with the integration of the Cloud API Registry, we’re excited to bring</span><strong style="vertical-align:baseline"> enhanced tool governance capabilities</strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> </span><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">to</strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> </span><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">Vertex AI Agent Builder</strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline">. With this latest update, administrators can now manage available tools for developers across your organization directly in </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/api-registry/docs/console"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">Vertex AI Agent Builder Console</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline">, and developers can leverage tools managed by the registry with a new </span><a href="https://google.github.io/adk-docs/tools/google-cloud/api-registry/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><code style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">ApiRegistry</code></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline">.</span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> </span></p>
<p><span style="vertical-align:baseline">With this, organizations can anchor agents in the embedded security and operational controls that they already use, enabling deploying and managing agents as a digital workforce.</span></p>
<p><span style="vertical-align:baseline">Following </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/more-ways-to-build-and-scale-ai-agents-with-vertex-ai-agent-builder?e=48754805?utm_source%3Dlinkedin"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">last month's expansion</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> of our </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/agent-builder?e=48754805&amp;hl=en"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">Agent Builder</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> platform, we are also introducing new capabilities across the entire agent lifecycle to help developers build faster using new ADK capabilities and visual tools, and scale with high performance through the expansion of Agent Engine services, including the general availability of support for sessions and memory. Read more below.</span></p>
<h3><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">1. Govern your tools with confidence</strong></h3>
<p><span style="vertical-align:baseline">Building a useful agent requires the agent to have access to the necessary tools. However, developers today spend a significant amount of time building their tools for each agent, resulting in duplicate work. This approach also presents challenges for administrators who want to control what data and tools agents can access. </span></p>
<p><span style="vertical-align:baseline">We are bringing enhanced tool governance with the integration of Cloud API Registry in the </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/api-registry/docs/console"><strong style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">Vertex AI Agent Builder Console</strong></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline">. This acts as a private registry that administrators can use to curate and govern a set of approved tools for developers to use across their organization, providing: </span></p>
<ul>
<li style="list-style-type:disc;vertical-align:baseline">
<p><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">Pre-built tools for Google services</strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline">: We recently </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/announcing-official-mcp-support-for-google-services?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">announced</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> MCP support for Google services like BigQuery and Google Maps, which will be available for use in Vertex AI Agent Builder.</span></p>
</li>
<li style="list-style-type:disc;vertical-align:baseline">
<p><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">Support for custom MCP servers:</strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> Unlock your entire API estate for the agentic age. Apigee now empowers you to </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/mcp-support-for-apigee?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">transform your existing managed APIs into custom MCP servers</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline">, bridging your established digital assets with modern AI workflows. Additionally, by bringing these tools from multiple clouds into </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/apigee/docs/apihub/what-is-api-hub"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">Apigee API hub</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline">, you help ensure your agent developers have instant and secure access to a curated catalog through the </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/api-registry/docs/overview"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">Cloud API Registry.</span></a></p>
</li>
<li style="list-style-type:disc;vertical-align:baseline">
<p><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">Enhanced tool management: </strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline">Administrators using the new experience in Vertex AI Agent Builder to view, govern, and manage tools can now ensure the right tools are available to developers in their organization.</span></p>
</li>
<li><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">Simplified tool access:</strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> For developers, </span><a href="https://google.github.io/adk-docs/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">Agent Development Kit (ADK)</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> introduces support of Cloud API Registry, introducing a new </span><code style="vertical-align:baseline">ApiRegistry</code><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> object to easily leverage managed tools.</span></li>
</ul></div></section><section class="QzPuud"><div><section><figure class="NEBdNd"><section class="PBkdHd DhGbH" jscontroller="SCGBie" jsaction="rcuQ6b:npT2md"><img class="JcsBte mZzdH ZOnyjc" src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/original_images/1_0yaFnYm.gif" alt="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/original_images/1_0yaFnYm.gif" jsname='P3Vluc' jsaction="click:HTIlC" loading="lazy"/><section class="glue-modal glue-modal--dark QHdDac" role="dialog" aria-modal="true"><img class="JcsBte mZzdH ZOnyjc" src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/original_images/1_0yaFnYm.gif" alt="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/original_images/1_0yaFnYm.gif" jsname='P3Vluc' jsaction="click:HTIlC" loading="lazy"/><button class="glue-modal__close-btn" tabindex="0" aria-label="Close this modal"></button></section></section></figure><div class="nRhiJb-cHYyed nRhiJb-DbgRPb-R6PoUb-ma6Yeb ZpqjUe"><div jsaction="rcuQ6b:npT2md" jscontroller="M0Q3Qb" data-is-cws-richtext="true" class=" "><p>The demo above showcases the new user journey for managing and governing tools directly within the Vertex AI Agent Builder Console</p></div></div></section></div></section><section class="Wy08Ac nRhiJb-qJTHM-OWXEXe-hJDwNd nRhiJb-DbgRPb-II5mzb-cGMI2b"><div jsaction="rcuQ6b:npT2md" jscontroller="M0Q3Qb" data-is-cws-richtext="true" class=" "><h3><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">2. Build your AI agents faster</strong></h3>
<p><span style="vertical-align:baseline">Last month, we released </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/vertex-ai/generative-ai/docs/models/gemini/3-pro"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">Gemini 3 Pro</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline">, our most intelligent model, to every developer and enterprise team. It’s the best model in the world for multimodal understanding, and our most powerful agentic model yet. With full compatibility with </span><a href="https://google.github.io/adk-docs/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">ADK</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline">, you can now build, test, and deploy powerful AI agents with greater reliability and confidence. We are introducing new capabilities to help you move from concept to interactive product:</span></p>
<ul>
<li><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">Full ADK support of Gemini 3 Pro and Flash: </strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline">ADK now fully supports </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/gemini-3-is-available-for-enterprise?e=48754805?utm_source%3Dlinkedin"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">Gemini 3 Pro</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> and </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/gemini-3-flash-for-enterprises?utm_source=instagram&amp;utm_medium=unpaidsoc&amp;utm_campaign=fy25q4-googlecloud-blog-ai-bio-no-brand-global&amp;utm_content=-&amp;utm_term=-&amp;e=48754805?utm_source%3Dlinkedin"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">Flash</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline">, allowing you to build reliable, production-ready agents. </span></li>
<li><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">ADK for TypeScript: </strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline">We are extending ADK support for </span><a href="https://github.com/google/adk-js" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">TypeScript</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline">, ensuring you can leverage the latest capabilities in ADK directly in whatever language you choose. </span></li>
<li><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">State management in ADK: </strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline">We've made significant improvements to our agentic </span><a href="https://google.github.io/adk-docs/sessions/state/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">state management</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> within ADK, which is the system for an AI agent to maintain context and memory during and across conversations. New improvements include: </span>
<ul>
<li><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">Recovery from failure</strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline">: If a conversation crashes due to an error, ADK now restores the state natively, requiring no additional work from the developer.</span></li>
<li><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">Continue with human-in-the-loop</strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline">: You can now pause for human input anywhere, even inside complex workflows. ADK automatically remembers exactly where the agent stopped and resumes immediately after approval, so you don't have to write extra code to track progress.</span></li>
<li><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">Rewind state and context: </strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline">Developers can now rewind to any point in the conversation and invalidate all interactions after that point so the user can remove the “polluted” context rather than send a new message. This allows users to try different approaches to solving a problem without having to open new sessions.</span></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">Interactions API integration:</strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> ADK and the Agent2Agent protocol (A2A) now support the new </span><a href="https://developers.googleblog.com/building-agents-with-the-adk-and-the-new-interactions-api/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">Interactions API</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline">, providing a consistent way to manage multimodal input/output (text, audio, visual) across your agents, simplifying integration with client applications.</span></li>
<li><a href="https://a2ui.org/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><strong style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">A2UI</strong></a><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">:</strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> Built on top of A2A protocol, </span><a href="https://developers.googleblog.com/introducing-a2ui-an-open-project-for-agent-driven-interfaces/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">A2UI</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> is an early-stage UI toolkit to facilitate LLM-generated UIs for remote agents. This allows you to enable agents to pass shared UI widgets and components directly to user-facing applications without the security risks and overhead of iframes or sending executable code, allowing you to build rich user experiences securely.</span></li>
</ul></div></section><section class="YNV64d"><section><div jsaction="rcuQ6b:npT2md" jscontroller="wJu6E" class="nRhiJb-aTv5jf glue-video__preview-container glue-video__preview-container--inline" style="vertical-align:baseline">You can start building today with </span><a href="https://github.com/google/adk-samples" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">adk-samples</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> on GitHub or on </span><a style="vertical-align:baseline">, a growing repository of curated agent samples, solutions, and tools designed to accelerate your development and support one-click deployment of your agents built with ADK. Access our </span><a href="https://googlecloudplatform.github.io/agent-starter-pack/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">Agent Starter Pack</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline">, a template collection that provides a production-ready foundation for building, testing, and deploying AI agents. </span></p>
<h3><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">3. Scale your AI agents effectively</strong></h3>
<p><span style="vertical-align:baseline">Once you’ve built your agent, the next challenge is going into a production environment. That’s why we continue to expand the managed services available in </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/agent-builder/agent-engine/overview"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">Agent Engine</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> to provide the core capabilities needed to scale your agents.</span></p>
<ul>
<li style="list-style-type:disc;vertical-align:baseline">
<p><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">Manage context with confidence:</strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> We are moving</span><strong style="vertical-align:baseline"> </strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline">Agent Engine sessions and memory bank to General Availability </span><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">(</strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline">GA</span><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">)</strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline">. You can now use Agent Engine to manage both short-term and long-term memory for your production workloads. This allows your agents to maintain context across different interactions, which is critical for delivering helpful, personalized responses at scale. This product is powered by </span><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2503.08026" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">Google Cloud AI Research’s novel research method (accepted by ACL 2025)</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline">, using a topic-based approach that sets a new standard for how agents learn and recall information.</span></p>
</li>
<li style="list-style-type:disc;vertical-align:baseline">
<p><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">Expanded regional support for Agent Engine services</strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline">: All Agent Engine services are now available in seven additional regions worldwide. To learn more, refer to the </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/agent-builder/locations"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">documentation</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline">.</span></p>
</li>
<li style="list-style-type:disc;vertical-align:baseline">
<p><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">Pricing updates for Agent Engine:</strong><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> We lowered pricing for the Agent Engine runtime and will begin billing for additional Agent Engine services starting on January 28, 2026. You can review the </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/vertex-ai/pricing?e=48754805#vertex-ai-agent-engine"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">Agent Engine pricing documentation</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> for additional detail and hypothetical agent cost scenarios.</span></p>
</li>
</ul>

<h3><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">How customers are achieving more with Agent Builder</strong></h3>
<p style="padding-left:40px"><span style="font-style:italic;vertical-align:baseline">&quot;Burns &amp; McDonnell uses Vertex AI Agent Builder to transform how organizational knowledge is applied across the enterprise. With Experience IQ, we are building an AI agent using ADK</span><strong style="vertical-align:baseline"> </strong><span style="font-style:italic;vertical-align:baseline">that turns decades of project data and employee experience into real-time, actionable intelligence. Vertex AI enables this innovation to scale responsibly by combining deterministic business rules with probabilistic reasoning, making AI a trusted operational capability — not just a productivity tool. This agent helps teams quickly identify the right experience, reduce manual effort in staffing and planning, and make higher-confidence decisions grounded in verified data. With Vertex AI, Burns &amp; McDonnell isn’t just managing knowledge — we are activating experience to drive faster, more confident decisions.&quot; </span><span style="vertical-align:baseline">- Matt Olson, Chief Innovation Officer, Burns &amp; McDonnell</span></p>
<p style="padding-left:40px"><span style="font-style:italic;vertical-align:baseline">“Payhawk uses Vertex AI Agent Builder to transform agents into financial assistants that truly ‘know’ our customers. Leveraging Memory Bank, we moved from stateless interactions to long-term context retention, allowing agents to recall user constraints and historical patterns with continuity. For example, our Financial Controller Agent now remembers habits like expensing small meals and auto-submits them, reducing submission time by over 50%. Similarly, our Travel Agent proactively applies preferences like aisle seats. This significantly drops cognitive load, allowing agents to anticipate needs based on past behavior rather than just reacting to prompts.”</span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> - Diyan Bogdanov, Principal Applied AI Engineer, Payhawk</span></p>
<p style="padding-left:40px"><span style="font-style:italic;vertical-align:baseline">"Gurunavi uses Vertex AI Agent Builder</span><strong style="font-style:italic;vertical-align:baseline"> </strong><span style="font-style:italic;vertical-align:baseline">to power 'UMAME!', an AI restaurant discovery app that leverages Agent Engine's Memory Bank to overcome a significant challenge: achieving a deep understanding of user context. Unlike conventional prompt-based systems, our agent leverages memory bank to remember a user's past actions, preferences, and temporal patterns to proactively present the best options. This eliminates the need for manual searches, creating a seamless experience. We project this context-aware capability will improve user experience by 30% or more. We view this memory function as a non-negotiable feature for helping everyone forge new culinary experiences together with AI.”</span><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> - Toshiaki Iwamoto, CTO, Gurunavi</span></p>
<p style="padding-left:40px"><span style="font-style:italic;vertical-align:baseline">“SeaArt Entertainment uses Vertex AI Agent Builder to personalize the creative experience for digital artists. Before Memory Bank, our AI agents could not reliably remember users’ preferences. For example, when users worked on complex multimodal art projects, they had to repeatedly explain the same details — like their favorite character styles or model choices — across sessions. After integrating Memory Bank, our agents are now able to recall past conversations, actions, and user preferences. We especially like that the agent can seamlessly remember context across sessions, making interactions feel more natural and personal." </span><span style="vertical-align:baseline">- Aleksei Savin, Lead of Multimodal AI Platform, SeaArt Entertainment</span></p>
<h3><strong style="vertical-align:baseline">Get started</strong></h3>
<p><span style="vertical-align:baseline">Vertex AI Agent Builder provides the unified platform to manage the entire agent lifecycle, helping you close the gap from prototype to a production-ready agent. To explore these new features, visit the updated </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/agent-builder/overview"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">Agent Builder documentation</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline"> and </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/agent-builder/release-notes"><span style="text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline">release notes</span></a><span style="vertical-align:baseline">.</span></p>

This guide provides the knowledge needed to go from an idea to prototype to scale, whether your goals are to automate tasks, enhance creativity, or launch entirely new user experiences for your \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca href\u003d\"https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/gemini-3-is-available-for-enterprise?e\u003d48754805?utm_source%3Dlinkedin\"\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eWe are extending ADK support for \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca href\u003d\"https://github.com/google/adk-js\" rel\u003d\"noopener\" style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e, ensuring you can leverage the latest capabilities in ADK directly in whatever language you choose. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eState management in ADK: \u003c/strong\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eWe've made significant improvements to our agentic \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca href\u003d\"https://google.github.io/adk-docs/sessions/state/\" rel\u003d\"noopener\" target\u003d\"_blank\"\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline\"\u003estate management\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e within ADK, which is the system for an AI agent to maintain context and memory during and across conversations. New improvements include: \u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eRecovery from failure\u003c/strong\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e: If a conversation crashes due to an error, ADK now restores the state natively, requiring no additional work from the developer.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eContinue with human-in-the-loop\u003c/strong\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e: You can now pause for human input anywhere, even inside complex workflows. ADK automatically remembers exactly where the agent stopped and resumes immediately after approval, so you don't have to write extra code to track progress.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eRewind state and context: \u003c/strong\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eDevelopers can now rewind to any point in the conversation and invalidate all interactions after that point so the user can remove the “polluted” context rather than send a new message. This allows users to try different approaches to solving a problem without having to open new sessions.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eInteractions API integration:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e ADK and the Agent2Agent protocol (A2A) now support the new \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca href\u003d\"https://developers.googleblog.com/building-agents-with-the-adk-and-the-new-interactions-api/\" rel\u003d\"noopener\" target\u003d\"_blank\"\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eInteractions API\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e, providing a consistent way to manage multimodal input/output (text, audio, visual) across your agents, simplifying integration with client applications.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href\u003d\"https://a2ui.org/\" rel\u003d\"noopener\" target\u003d\"_blank\"\u003e\u003cstrong style\u003d\"text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eA2UI\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cstrong style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e Built on top of A2A protocol, \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca href\u003d\"https://developers.googleblog.com/introducing-a2ui-an-open-project-for-agent-driven-interfaces/\" rel\u003d\"noopener\" target\u003d\"_blank\"\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eA2UI\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e is an early-stage UI toolkit to facilitate LLM-generated UIs for remote agents. This allows you to enable agents to pass shared UI widgets and components directly to user-facing applications without the security risks and overhead of iframes or sending executable code, allowing you to build rich user experiences securely.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e"]]],[null,null,null,null,null,null,["https://www.youtube.com/watch?v\u003dNauK8YMiJEE",[null,"Above is a demo showcasing A2UI in action where the user uploads a photo, a remote agent uses Gemini to understand it, and dynamically generates a custom form using A2UI for the specific needs of the customer."],null,["https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/maxresdefault_gjLbdeV.max-1300x1300.jpg","https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/maxresdefault_gjLbdeV.max-1100x1100.jpg 1060w, https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/maxresdefault_gjLbdeV.max-1300x1300.jpg 1280w"," 1060px,  1280px","https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/maxresdefault_gjLbdeV.max-1300x1300.jpg"]]],[null,null,[null,[null,"\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eYou can start building today with \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca href\u003d\"https://github.com/google/adk-samples\" rel\u003d\"noopener\" target\u003d\"_blank\"\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eadk-samples\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e on GitHub or on \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca href\u003d\"http://console.cloud.google.com/vertex-ai/agents/agent-garden\"\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eVertex AI Agent Garden\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e, a growing repository of curated agent samples, solutions, and tools designed to accelerate your development and support one-click deployment of your agents built with ADK. That’s why we continue to expand the managed services available in \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca href\u003d\"https://docs.cloud.google.com/agent-builder/agent-engine/overview\"\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eAgent Engine\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e to provide the core capabilities needed to scale your agents.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli style\u003d\"list-style-type:disc;vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eManage context with confidence:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e We are moving\u003c/span\u003e\u003cstrong style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e \u003c/strong\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eAgent Engine sessions and memory bank to General Availability \u003c/span\u003e\u003cstrong style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e(\u003c/strong\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eGA\u003c/span\u003e\u003cstrong style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e)\u003c/strong\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e. You can now use Agent Engine to manage both short-term and long-term memory for your production workloads. This allows your agents to maintain context across different interactions, which is critical for delivering helpful, personalized responses at scale. This product is powered by \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca href\u003d\"https://arxiv.org/pdf/2503.08026\" rel\u003d\"noopener\" target\u003d\"_blank\"\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"text-decoration:underline;vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eGoogle Cloud AI Research’s novel research method (accepted by ACL 2025)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e, using a topic-based approach that sets a new standard for how agents learn and recall information.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli style\u003d\"list-style-type:disc;vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003eExpanded regional support for Agent Engine services\u003c/strong\u003e\u003cspan style\u003d\"vertical-align:baseline\"\u003e: All Agent Engine services are now available in seven additional regions worldwide.
